12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江大庆市被迫流离失所的法轮功学员。丈夫白玉福是原大庆市石油管理局测井公司武保科科长；妻子张立新，原大庆石油管理局物业二公司乘风热力分公司职工。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，白玉福和张立新开始修炼法轮功，按真、善、忍标准做好人。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，白玉福、张立新夫妇多次被中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，白玉福、张立新夫妇在辽宁省阜新市彰武县被警方抓捕，后刑事拘留、批捕、起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被彰武县法院视频开庭。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日获悉，白玉福被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，张立新被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。张立新刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，张立新在阜新市新地看守所被迫害致脑出血，经抢救，保住了生命，肌肉已开始萎缩，保外就医被拒。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/24/2022-2-24.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/24/2022-2-24.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张梦颖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">全国出嫁女维权代表人物。河北省石家庄市高新区宋营镇南辛庄村人。的张梦颖女士，是结婚后户口没有迁出，却被所谓村规民俗的男女不平的陋俗，剥夺了集体经济组织成员权利，也是全国百万“出嫁女”群体的维权代表，其诉求已历经<span lang="EN-US">16</span>年之久，至今未得到解决，维权多年被当地政府公安机关打压。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">15</span>点 左右，一群自称是石家庄市公安局的人，强行撬开张梦颖张梦颖的家门，并控制其家属后将张梦颖带走。到昨晚<span lang="EN-US">21</span>点多的时候，这群警察又返回张梦颖女士家里抄家，将电脑等物品抄走。据张梦颖的朋友说，第二天上午辖区派出所打电话给家人，说张梦颖已经被拘留，没有说什么理由，或什么罪名。石家庄当局抓捕张梦颖女士，疑与其在全国“两会”期间“妇女节”前夕，向参会代表、委员们吁请中国政府兑现<span lang="EN-US">40</span>多年来“生男生女一个样”的承诺，及同时要求全国人大常委会取消河北省王东峰、石家庄市委书记张超超的全国人大代表资格有关。明显有公报私仇、打击报复嫌疑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_33.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_33.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张明毅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省南京市玄武区法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生。，江苏省金陵石化建安公司职工，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月开始修炼法轮大法，身心受益。后曾三次在洗脑班、两次在精神病院被关押迫害，一次被非法劳教二年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在单位办公室被警察绑架带走，随后被抄家，抄走了打印机及真相资料等私人物品，后一直被非法关押。直到<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现被关押在苏州监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张慕杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，北京法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生，祖籍北京延庆，孤身一人居住在北京大兴区。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日清晨，张慕杰被闯入家中的清源路派出所吴姓警察抓捕。警察抢走法轮功台历九十本左右，内夹真相期刊等。张慕杰被关押在大兴看守所。清源派出所吴姓警察对张慕杰进一步构陷和批捕。张慕杰已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被大兴区法院秘密非法判刑四年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张乃君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省鞍山市人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功遭当局长期打压迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，当其在鞍山市铁西区兴盛街道附近粘贴法轮功资料时，遭到铁西区兴盛街道办事处工作人员白英涛的恶意举报，遂被鞍山市铁西区兴盛派出所警方很快以涉嫌宣传邪教罪抓捕，次日被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日已被鞍山市铁西区检察院以同罪名正式批捕。被羁押于鞍山市第一看守所。后取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日又遭抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被庭审。刑期未知。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张盼成：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1995</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，甘肃省庆阳市合水县人，网名为“子慕予兮”，中国西北农村长大留守儿童，前北京大学保安，正义公民，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早年出生于甘肃农村，是典型的留守儿童；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾以公民身份表达自己的意愿；在辞去北京大学保安工作之后，曾放胆自拍视频，发政治主张，称已为民主“做好了牺牲的准备”；被捕前，曾在视频中表示，不同意中国政府将<span lang="EN-US">600</span>亿美元未经法定程序送<span lang="EN-US">(</span>外国）人，要求言论自由，声援被失踪的董瑶琼、华涌、佳士工人和原北大学生岳昕等人，以及进学习班的百万新疆同胞；曾在视频中引用宋代名将文天祥的诗句“人生自古谁无死，留取丹心照汗青”，并说自己对国家有深沉的爱；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，被抓捕刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被北京市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；审讯中，拒绝写保证书，并拒绝给律师签委托书；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其案在北京西城区法院开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被北京市西城区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因其在网上发布一段在甘肃山村老家里录制的视频，谴责中共暴行，表达心声称“凛凛寒冬终将过去，春天马上要来临”，随后被当地警方带走，后知又被当地合县检察院转正式批捕，被关押在甘肃省庆阳市合水县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，知其已被甘肃省合水县法院一审秘判，但其家人未获判决书；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日本网获悉，其似被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。目前在甘肃省武都监狱（甘肃省武都区吉石坝武都监狱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">746000</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/3-3.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/3-3.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张鹏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西咸阳市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">35</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">岁左右，本科学历，不论是在家乡还是在单位都是受人称赞的热心青年。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">咸阳市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员</span>张鹏、王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏因为向淳化县民众发放真相资料，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月先后在各自的住所被淳化县公安局警察抓捕抄家。张鹏、王钰超（<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁左右）<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底在咸阳市住处被警察绑架，电脑、打印机等设备被抢走。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位法轮功学员被关押在咸阳淳化县看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均已被判刑，其中张鹏判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏约为<span lang="EN-US">5</span>至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年不等，刑期不详。张鹏刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html#zip3</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张鹏柱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省本溪市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，邓玉林、张莉敏、张鹏柱、胡林、杨丽威五位法轮功学员，向当地民众讲清法轮功被迫害真相，去桓仁县散发法轮功资料，被本溪市国保支队、桓仁县国保大队和普乐堡派出所共计抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，邓玉林、胡林被关押在桓仁县看守所，张鹏柱被关押于桓仁县拘留所，杨丽威、张莉敏被关押在本溪市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，胡林被转往沈阳法库县看守所关押。胡林最终被判刑两年。从被抓捕开始，胡林一直在绝食抵制迫害，在被迫害的生命垂危的情况下，被法库县看守所走后门强行送往沈阳康家山监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被沈阳康家山监狱迫害致死。本案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日宣判：邓玉林和杨丽威<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，各罚金二万元，张莉敏<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万五千元，张鹏柱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金一万元。张鹏柱刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午集团副总经理、温泉度假村经理。孙大午案受害人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：张平被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张强：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，辽宁省营口市人，<span lang="EN-US">89</span>六四亲历者，无身份证黑户人，前广州市某美国贸易公司重要职员，网络活跃人士<span lang="EN-US">,</span>社会热点事件关注者，民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年，张强曾就读于华南理工大学化工机械系高分子机械专业；<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月毕业之际，却因参与<span lang="EN-US">89</span>学运，要出门上街时被院系领导拦下，随后以“学习成绩不好”为由被学校开除，并其在校户籍亦被该校联合派出所偷偷注销，自此，使之成为一个彻底的无身份证黑户人（又称“隐形人”），以致长期不能到正规单位工作、不能乘坐火车、飞机，无法办理结婚登记，以及所有凡与身份证件相关的事宜都无法成行或着办成；之后，其曾为此将广州市公安局告上法庭，该案曾两次开庭审理，但都以其无身份证而被拒进入法庭参加庭审；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，因张强曾在朋友圈和微信群里发信息质疑了当地警局某领导的死因，遂被广东省广州市海珠区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，又被广州市海珠区检察院亦同罪名予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案被海珠区警方移送至海珠区检察院审查起诉，期间，延长审查起诉期限一次；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案在广州市海珠区法院开庭审理；据悉，检察院建议对其量刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前张强被羁押于广州市海珠区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_10.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_10.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张勤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">上海法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，家住上海市徐汇区，原是上海市胜德塑料有限公司的技术骨干，曾任总工程师、质监科科长等职务。一九九四年九月开始修炼法轮。张勤因为坚持信仰曾经两次被判刑，刑期分别为<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，还被劳教迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张勤又遭逮捕抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日下午，张勤被上海奉贤区法院庭审、判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，借口是“累犯重判”。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张勤：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1942</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日张勤被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张清香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张任飞<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，张任飞等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括张任飞在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。张任飞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省辛集市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁。家住辛集市前营乡八里邱村，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，他送孙子上学以后回家，被和睦井乡派出所的警察抓捕。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前在唐山某监狱中继续遭受关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁，辽宁省大连市沙河口区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚九点左右，张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波四人因发真相资料，分别被国保和民权派出所绑架。在张仁光家抄走大量耗材。后全送姚家看守所。大连市沙河口区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日庭审法轮功学员张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波，并判张仁光<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、勒索罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张瑞君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东淄博市法轮功学员。五十多岁，新华书店退休职工，家住淄博市高新区四宝山镇。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年三月十九日左右，张瑞君被淄博市桓台县国保跨区抓捕，被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，桓台县国保对她拘留、查体，并批捕。警察强迫家人给张瑞君办健康码后，在体检不合格的情况下，将她关押在淄博市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张瑞君被二次开庭，是视频开庭。在视频中，家人看到她已被迫害得非常严重。原本身体健康的她，说话时，反应迟钝，精神萎靡不振，走路都成问题。她的孩子了解到张瑞君睡眠、吃饭都相当差。由于体检有传染病，她被单独关押在一间屋里，不与任何人接触、说话。第二次开庭后，张瑞君被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。她不服判决，继续上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，家属得知，她已被送入济南女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/14/%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E5%BC%A0%E7%91%9E%E5%90%9B%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E5%85%A5%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E5%A5%B3%E5%AD%90%E7%9B%91%E7%8B%B1-440043.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/14/%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E5%BC%A0%E7%91%9E%E5%90%9B%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E5%85%A5%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E5%A5%B3%E5%AD%90%E7%9B%91%E7%8B%B1-440043.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张少杰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，河南省南乐县人，前河南省南乐县基督教三自爱国运动委员会主席、基督教协会会长，第九届南乐县政协委员，南乐县基督教会牧师，中国在押良心犯。长期以来，因其身为牧师，经常帮助弱势群体维权解难，尤其是当信徒的合法权益受到侵害时，均想法给予及时的帮助与维权，随在当地备受信徒的喜爱，但这种行为却与政府某些人的利益发生冲突，随遭到当局的强烈不满和忌恨；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被南乐县警方在无任何法律手续的前提下强行从教会带走，其两个胞妹在众人的陪同下前去公安局要人，也被警察强行带走，其余人等亦遭警方堵截和殴打，之后才得知张少杰已被当地警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，又被追加涉嫌“妨害公务罪”予以批捕，但在起诉书中又显示将“妨害公务罪”变更为“诈骗罪”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，终被河南省南乐县法院以“诈骗罪”和“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。此前曾先后被羁押在河南省南乐县看守所和濮阳市看守所；目前在河南省新乡市河南第二监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张盛全：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员。重庆市高新区石桥铺人。他原在石桥铺交易城做生意，公平交易，童叟无欺。张盛全曾屡遭中共迫害，他曾被非法劳教两年，在西山坪劳教所遭受过多种酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日重庆<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名法轮功学员张盛全、李嘉惠、李玉华、高洪伟、秦雪美，被抓捕两年多，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获悉已经被判刑。张盛全、李嘉惠，被枉判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；李玉华<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元，监外执行；高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；秦雪美<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。张盛全刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张淑萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东聊城市东昌府区名法轮功学员。张淑萍、王芹<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被聊城市东昌府区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>、国保大队、柳园派出所警察等抄家。王芹被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月左右被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。张淑萍的电动小汽车被安装了监控定位装置，在修车时被发现。张淑萍于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月上旬在高速路口被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底左右被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。王芹、张淑萍一直被关押在市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底左右被转送济南女子监狱关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/25/2021-9-25.html#zip1"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/25/2021-9-25.html#zip1</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张淑琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江伊春市法轮功学员，女，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">，家住伊春市伊春区，在伊春经营一家旅店。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日当地警方对张淑琴经营的旅店进行搜查，并以「利用×教组织破坏法律实施罪」将张淑琴刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，将张淑琴批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日伊美区法院对张淑琴开庭审理。张淑琴本人没有到法庭现场，是在看守所以视频方式出庭。律师为张淑琴做了无罪辩护。张淑琴女儿刘春莉也为母亲做了无罪辩护。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张水兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日生，云岭通信器材公司退休职工。张水兰<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年曾经遭受<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年冤狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日散发法轮功真相资料遭恶人诬告，被昆明市盘龙区东华派出所警察抓捕、非法抄家，抢走平板计算机一台，及大法书籍、数据等私人物品。后张水兰被昆明市西山区检察院起诉，云南省昆明市西山区法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日对昆明市法轮功学员张水兰判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10000</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张素英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏淮安市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，张素英<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日左右被淮安<span lang="EN-US">610</span>抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，张素英被清江浦区法院开庭， 一位维权律师出庭做无罪辩护。绑架、非法关押大半年，被淮安市清江浦区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。张素英老人已要求上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张树德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，哈尔滨市双城区新兴乡人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。自幼练习和笃信法轮功。哈尔滨工业大学毕业后，曾应聘于大连理工设计院，后外派到盘锦市高新技术产业开发区工作，是个诚实、可信、敬业的好青年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因居住证到期，张树德到所在地的兴隆台区兴盛派出所办理顺延手续时，当身份证录入相关信息时，警察问他有什么信仰，他称其信仰法轮功，随被拒绝办理居住证，并被威胁要对他调查。三天后，其居室遭搜查，本人被传唤做笔录。<span lang="EN-US"> 6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被双手戴着手铐非法送到盘锦市中心医院检查身体，然后就被强行刑拘于盘锦看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，他被盘锦市公安局兴隆台区分局正式逮捕，并将其案移交到兴隆台区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，检察院案将其案卷移交到兴隆台区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其案被盘锦市兴隆台区法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，张树德被该法院一审枉法重判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。其不服上诉。其所在家乡的亲友得知其被冤判后，立刻决定伸出援手征签营救，同乡的父老乡亲们在极短的时间里，亲自填写上自己的名字或按下红手印，呼吁无罪释放张树德回家，目前已有<span lang="EN-US">1744</span>人签名声援。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张顺新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆喀什地区泽普县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁，在中共对法轮功持续至今近二十年的迫害中，他因修炼法轮功在<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，但他挺过来了。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚十点左右，张顺新被塔西南石油基地公安局（隶属于泽普县公安局）警察冯海洋骗到派出所后，再次被绑架关押抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，新疆喀什地区公安局警察到法轮功学员张顺新家通知亲属，张顺新现被关在农三师图木舒克市盖米里克监狱。亲属这才知道张顺新于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并在亲属、律师不在场的情况下秘密宣判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">澳门居民。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，珠海王家婚礼教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛（澳门居民）被捕。数个月后，珠海市香洲区检察院以“诈骗罪”起诉。控方指魏小妹、李炳新及张涛涉嫌诈骗信徒奉献款，购买房产，构成诈骗罪。据知情人士披露，当局的指控缺乏有力证据，难以成立。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，香洲区民族宗教事务局取缔该教会，并扣留该教会近五十台电脑<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，当局出动数十名公安，拘捕该教会十多名信徒，经过连续审讯及威胁，信徒被迫写下不利于教会领袖的证词。警方最终以诈骗罪刑事拘留该教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛。据知情人士披露，该案由珠海市政法委督办。当局先以“邪教罪”调查此案，但因查无实据，又改为“诈骗罪”问罪，这明显是一起宗教案件。目前，广东珠海王家婚礼教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛（澳门居民）三人，被珠海市香洲区检察院以“诈骗罪”起诉至法院，指当事人诈骗奉献款，上述三人面临判刑。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张廷福：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁老人张廷福在达州下火车，被达州车站派出所拦截扣押后刑事拘留，问其原因，是重庆上清寺派出所将张廷福上传为网上追逃人员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日重庆维权人士张廷福，被重庆市公安局渝中区分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑拘，现羁押在渝中区看守所。家属经多方投诉后，才于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日拿到刑事拘留通知书，张廷福也从达州转至重庆渝中区看守所，得知成为逃犯的原因，是派出所以其涉嫌寻衅滋事罪，上传为网上追逃。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张廷祥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">贵州省安顺市平坝县新艺厂（<span lang="EN-US">170</span>厂）法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始迫害法轮功后，张廷祥坚持修炼，多次被迫害，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，张廷祥被贵州省贵安新区<span lang="EN-US">30</span>个警察入室抓捕、抄家，抢走电脑、书籍、手机等几箱子私人物品，还劫走了张廷祥个人现金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万元。张廷祥被关押在平坝看守所，后被关押在安顺市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被贵阳市南明区法院判刑：张廷祥获刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">张伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，家住东港市。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，丹东市委、政法委、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”与丹东市公安局秘密策划，经过长期电话监控以及各种监控手段、跟踪监视，对丹东市公安系统统一部署，丹东国保支队警察倾巢出动，加上直属公安分局以及法轮功学员所在地公安派出所为主力，合计至少一千几百人参与此次抓捕。此次行动，东港市<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员被抓捕。张伟也遭抓捕和抄家，抢走法轮书籍、资料若干、笔记本电脑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>台、打印机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台、几部手机。张伟被关进丹东看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，辽宁丹东地区东港市法院对<span lang="EN-US">11</span>名法轮功学员非法庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，东港市法院对法轮功学员下达判决。张伟被非法判重刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，现非法关押在辽宁女子监狱<span lang="EN-US">1</span>监区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>小队。张伟一直坚持炼功，曾多次被打骂、体罚、强制“转化”，张伟曾绝食反迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张文斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">原籍山东、原定今年大学毕业。因<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在微信实名公开发布“习近平下课”、“共产党下课”视频后，其微信被封杀，后又遭强迫失踪，目前处于失联状态。此前他曾因言获罪被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天。张文斌说，自己挺身而出，武汉肺炎疫情是导火索。而这段矛头指向习近平的视频使他又遭遇了强迫失踪。目前没有进一步的信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张文和：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，北京市通州区人，回族，<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁以前信仰伊斯兰教，<span lang="EN-US">51</span>岁以后皈依基督教，早年曾为北京花丝镶嵌厂、北京玉器厂职工，“张文和工艺品有限公司”创办人和经营者，<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-1979</span>年时期“西单民主墙运动”（简称“民主墙运动”）参与者，政治异议人士，民主人权活动家，中国在押政治犯。早年曾经历文化大革命十年浩劫磨难，小学三年级及被迫辍学，自此被定性为资本家的狗崽子而备受凌弱和不公；<span lang="EN-US">1979</span>年，曾因参与“民主墙运动”而遭北京当局刑拘<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，且刑拘期间受尽酷刑折磨；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代，为谋生计和筹集款项，曾开办“张文和工艺品有限公司”，其工艺品因质量精美优秀幸得被海湾伊斯兰国家博物馆收藏；之后，又因其乐善好施，随曾多次为清真寺捐款，并变卖其在通州区的三间房屋，将所得款项全部捐助给回民孩子用于阿拉伯语的学习；此期间，因追求民主人权理念而积极参与维权活动，曾<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次被北京当局送进精神病医院，接受惨无人道的人权迫害；近年来，因其放胆言论，呼唤<span lang="EN-US">"</span>颜色革命<span lang="EN-US">"</span>、倡导<span lang="EN-US">"</span>三民主义<span lang="EN-US">"</span>和<span lang="EN-US">"</span>新兴中会<span lang="EN-US">"</span>，呼吁中共与民主力量以及联合国为政治改革举行三方会谈而备受当局注目和敌视；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因不堪遭受中共政府愈加疯狂的逼迫而被迫前往巴林王国避难，但同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因其签证过期被捕，并被关在当地警局，之后即被遣返回国；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其再被北京市通州区中仓派出所警方带走，当天即被关进精神病院，并不许家属探视；其妻王素娥为此立即成立“营救张文和”群组，呼吁社会正义人士对其丈予以高度关注，同时，剃发明志，誓言维权到底；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，终于知其被关具体地址，但警方拒透其一切具体细节，只称<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日要做司法鉴定，结果得出后或被移转其他地方；据悉，其曾自曝被拘押在北京市公安局看守所期间，曾惨遭警方酷刑虐待，被狱警按在地上，从背后戴上“紧铐”，并将其头套上防毒面具，后又被上“死铐”，昼夜戴“背铐”<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个多月，直至被刑拘关押看守所<span lang="EN-US">19</span>个月后，再被送到北京市延庆监狱中的精神病医院继续关押长达<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，且历次被关精神病院，历次被强迫大量吃药，导致其身心伤害极大。目前被羁押于北京市通州区精神病医院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张文涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西南昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份，南昌市西湖区公安分局与东湖区公安分局联合，成立了迫害法轮功学员的专案组。他们通过摄像头查找后进行抓捕、抄家，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日逐一抓捕了张莉、江兰英、张文涛、胡水英、陈宝芝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，江西省南昌市西湖区法院判法轮功学员张文涛<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US"> 2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">张文英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，贵州省黔东南苗族侗族自治州（简称黔东南州）凯里市人，侗族（需再核实），基督徒，黔东南州凯里市基督复临安息日教会神职人员，聚会点负责人及长老，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代初成立基督复临安息日教会聚会点以来，因一直作为教会长老热心服侍教会并照顾信徒的一切事工活动，随被众信徒广为喜爱及信任；但因其所属教会拒不认同也不接受中共当局认可的“三自教会”管理，属于地下家庭教会<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余年，虽早已向贵州省宗教局提交教会聚会点合法申请，但始终未获审批，故遭贵州当局在意识形态上的严苛管理；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，又因其教会聚会点信徒不断增多，教会势力日渐强大，所以很快引起贵州省黔东南州当局关注与恐慌，并刻意成立项目组，对其聚会点进行全面侦查；之后，其被黔东南州凯里市警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘，自此失联，另有<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名教会神职人员亦被以“同案犯”抓捕刑拘；后其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均被黔东南州凯里市检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其因聚会点申请未被国家审批，众信徒所交奉献款均属于诈骗款，故而其行为属于违法；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案被当地凯里市法院一审以“诈骗罪”统一宣判，其因是教会长老而被枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月；另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位神职人员亦被枉判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>—<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年不等刑期；其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人不服判决，已向黔东南州中级法院提起上诉，二审正在等待中。目前被羁押于黔东南州凯里市看守所（贵州省<span lang="EN-US">/</span>黔东南苗族侗族自治州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>凯里市<span lang="EN-US">/</span>永乐路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">556099</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张五洲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">人权捍卫者、湖北籍、家住广东清远市。张五洲是被关进广州白云区看守所死亡的张六毛的姐姐。张五洲为了给弟弟的不明死亡讨回公道受到打压，开始关注公益和参与一些民主、人权活动。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，广州女律师孙世华在广州荔湾区华林派出所办案时，受到该所民警殴打并遭脱衣检查侮辱。随行的张五洲和梁颂基作为目击者，在网上公开为孙世华作证。广州警方为此报复，以“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕了张五洲和梁颂基。后梁颂基被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半和张五洲<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。张五洲女士于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日当天，前往广州著名风景区白云山，在山上栏杆上打出横幅，上书“勿忘六世，撤回恶法”、“女律师被殴目击证人”等字样，以此纪念<span lang="EN-US">31</span>年前的六四事件，以及反对中共两会刚刚通过的香港国安法的实施。张五洲把该活动拍照及视频发微信朋友圈和其它平台发布后，翌日（<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日）下午<span lang="EN-US">14</span>时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分，广东清远市公安局清城区分局石角派出所以张五洲“涉嫌扰乱公共秩序”为由将其清远市家中传唤带走，随后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日来警方又来抄家。后狱中遭受极其残暴的酷刑虐待。张五洲案于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在清远市清城区法院开庭，未当庭宣判。张五洲在被法院开庭<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后宣判，以寻衅滋事罪、妨碍公务罪被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，合并执行<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张希明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市东丽区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日上午九点三十分，天津市东丽区分局警察、国保大队便衣、军粮城派出所警察共十几个人，闯入张希明家中，强行非法抄家，并抓捕了张希明与他母亲刘玉红。当天下午五点，警察把刘玉红放回家，当晚把张希明关押到东丽区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，军粮城派出所两个警察给刘玉红送来张希明被刑事拘留的通知书。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底被开庭，后获悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁左右，大连市中山区人，原中山区青云小学教师，法轮功学员，良心犯。因信仰法轮功并起诉江泽民，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，被送洗脑班<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在学校上班时间又被大连市国保与民主广场派出所警方联合绑架抓走，家被查抄，电脑及相关法轮功资料等均被搜走。其丈夫孙俊区派出所问询，已被扣押，后得知夫妇二人均被关押在大连市姚家看守所羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其被大连中山区检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年被大连市中山区法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月。其不服提起上诉，大连市中级法院未经二审即对她维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，张霞被送往辽宁省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张宪军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市双城区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，张宪军、徐艳与法轮功学员李慧敏<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人在双城区北二道街大修厂楼附近，往私家车上放突破网络封锁的法轮功二维码卡片，被不明真相人诬告，随被双城南街刑侦大队进行审讯，录口供，且家遭查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，张宪军、徐艳夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人又被东风派出所抓捕。隔离<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后，张宪军被关押在双城看守所，徐艳被关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所。之后一直没有<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人消息 。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知张宪军、徐艳夫妇在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被判刑，张宪军被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，徐艳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人提已出上诉。现在是否到监狱服刑，没有确切消息。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/14/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E5%B8%82%E5%8F%8C%E5%9F%8E%E5%8C%BA%E5%BC%A0%E5%AE%AA%E5%86%9B%E3%80%81%E5%BE%90%E8%89%B3%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430771.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/14/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E5%B8%82%E5%8F%8C%E5%9F%8E%E5%8C%BA%E5%BC%A0%E5%AE%AA%E5%86%9B%E3%80%81%E5%BE%90%E8%89%B3%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430771.html</span></a></span><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张小麦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原名陈煜，浙江临海市基督徒。张小麦</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈煜）因在开设网上书店“小麦书房”销售基督教书籍</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">,</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被捕</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">,</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">在张小麦于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被中共当局以「网上销售非法境外宗教出版物」被捕后，公安部曾通报全国，要求各地国保根据从「小麦书房」搜到的发货订单接触收货人，就其购买书籍的取向和「当地非法宗教活动的情况」进行取证，有上万人被问询。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">27</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日一审判决，以非法经营罪判</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑。并处以罚金</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万，所扣押</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12864</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本书予以销毁。判决书同时裁定，被告除了被罚</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元外，还须追缴售书违法所得的</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元上缴国库，无法追缴的，由被告退赔，并须予判决生效后十天内缴纳。这是对传播基督教的基督徒的赤裸裸的镇压。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，二审维持原判。刑期至：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2026</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/7.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/7.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张小平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛阳维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号，洛阳政府为了修建西环路，在程序不合法的情况下，对张小平家宅基地上的房屋进行了强拆，张小平也因此被逼自学法律，走上了依法维权抗争之路。张小平通过信息公开、行政诉讼等法律途径获取了一些关于修建道路的政府信息，通过对这些信息的分析，发现了前洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身违法修建西环路造成至少<span lang="EN-US">1</span>亿元国有资产流失的事实。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，张小平就这一事实，实名向驻河南中央第一巡视组<span lang="EN-US">65</span>号邮寄了一封《举报信》，此信查询单显示<span lang="EN-US">3.28</span>日已经妥投。巡视组不但没有保护张小平举报人的身份，此举更是将张小平暴露在被举报人的眼皮之下，被打击报复也是迟早之事； 因为举报的事情，张小平接到过威胁电话。关于泄漏举报人信息的问题，张小平通过新浪微博发声质疑，并要求相关部门查处。其最后一个博文发于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，结果，违法人员没得到查处，举报人却被抓了进去。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，洛阳公民张小平疑因举报厅级干部被刑事拘留，其丈夫张智斌行政拘留。原因疑是他们向中央巡视组举报原洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身（正厅级干部）。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张小平被洛阳公安局南昌路分局（电话<span lang="EN-US">0379-64316110</span>）抓捕；涉嫌罪名是“寻衅滋事”，<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日早被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被批捕。羁押在洛阳看守所。后无进一步信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张小琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆涪陵区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，女。张小琴<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在涪陵讲法轮功时被构陷，被涪陵区国保警察抓捕、抄家。抄走电脑、打印机、大法书籍等物品，后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张小琴被批捕。被绑架构陷大半年后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被重庆南川区法院庭审，后悉被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张秀芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林农安县法轮功学员。女、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员。此次抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的。此次被抓捕的法轮功学员有</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张秀芝、高晓歧、蔡玉英、吴冬梅、于姣茹、单为和、赵秀兰、孙秀英、张敬元、孙凤仙、冯立齐、吕相富、董秀辉等<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">22</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。他们被抓捕、构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：张秀芝被判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张雪春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">微信名海燕，维权人士。于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被沈阳市和平分局以（聚众犹乱社会秩序）罪刑拘，目前关押在沈阳市第一看守所，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日批捕。张雪春家人委托的代理律师向大家征集在北京最高检察院、最高人民法院的目击证人，证明张雪春在按照我国相关法律法规，依法有序向最高人民检察院，最高人民法院，提出司法改革建议过程中，没有任何违法行为，更没有任何犯罪行为以事实，然后走正常法律程序，还当事人以清白，请大家自愿报名，为张雪春出庭作证，证明其当事人无罪。已有上百人目击者报名上庭作证。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张雪莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">甘肃酒泉市瓜州县法轮功学员。此前，张雪莲因信仰真、善、忍，曾被吉林省长春黑嘴子劳教所劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，被无理剥夺工作，并曾被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，在甘肃女子监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，张雪莲，被国保警察抓捕到敦煌看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，在没有通知家人的情况下，敦煌法院去看守所，宣读对张雪莲的判决结果：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张艳会：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height:
